= Engineering Model Go Repository Design
:toc:
:toclevels: 2
:sectnums:

== Introduction

This <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL,architecture models>> the engineering-model-go repository as a model-driven toolchain.
It captures authored functional intent, export surfaces, and verification-oriented traceability.
The model is intended to guide implementation work in this repository using stable IDs and support paths.

=== Scope and Assumptions

- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_GROUP,Functional Groups>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FUNCTIONAL_UNIT,Functional Units>> are the stable authored design backbone.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_RUNTIME_ELEMENT,Runtime elements>> and <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_CODE_ELEMENT,code elements>> are inferred from available IaC, deployment, and source artifacts.
- Inferred coverage is evidence-driven and may be partial when source metadata is missing.
- <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,Requirements>> and reference indexes are provided for traceability, not as primary narrative flow.

== How To Read This Document

This document is intentionally split into two layers:

1. Concept layer: functional and view-specific architecture narratives for human understanding.
2. Evidence layer: generated requirement traceability and inferred reference indexes.

Read in this order:

1. Architecture Intent View: stable authored architecture intent and ownership boundaries.
2. Communication / Deployment / Security Views: viewpoint-specific operational behavior.
3. Traceability View: requirement mapping, evidence coverage, and confidence.
4. Reference Appendix: supporting reference IDs and inferred-source links.

++++
<style>
a[href^="#REF_"],

|===
|View |Authored Status |Authored Status Explanation |Units in Scope |Direct Evidence Coverage |Gap Count |Heuristic Confidence |Heuristic Basis
|Architecture Intent View (`VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT`)
|in-review
|Initial repository self-model with stable top-level domains; implementation details will be expanded iteratively.
|13
|13
|0
|high
|Defaults authored units to covered; use authoredStatus as the primary publication signal.
|Security View (`VIEW-SECURITY`)
|in-review
|Security scope starts from MCP boundary and export-validation supply chain paths.
|12
|12
|9
|high
|Counts a unit as covered when explicit authored attack-vector mapping exists.
|Traceability View (`VIEW-TRACEABILITY`)
|in-review
|Traceability scope is seeded and will be tightened as requirements are added.
|10
|10
|10
|high
|Counts a unit as covered when direct inferred runtime or code evidence exists.
|State Lifecycle View (`VIEW-STATE-LIFECYCLE`)
|draft
|Captures model validity and artifact freshness lifecycle behavior.
|0
|0
|0
|n/a
|Lifecycle heuristic is currently basic; treat authoredStatus as primary signal.
|Interaction Flow View (`VIEW-INTERACTION-FLOW`)
|draft
|Core implementation workflow is captured to guide model-driven repository changes.
|3
|3
|0
|high
|Flow heuristic is step/branch-oriented; treat authoredStatus plus projection completeness as the primary signal.
|===

== Terms and Definitions

|===
|Term |Definition
|[[REF_ENGMODEL_EM_ACTOR]]<<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_ACTOR,actor>> (EM-ACTOR)
|A person or operational role that interacts with functional units.
|[[REF_CATALOG_ACT_AI_AGENT]]<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_ACT_AI_AGENT,ai agent>> (ACT-AI-AGENT)
|Consumes MCP and AI JSON outputs to plan and execute model-guided edits. Aliases:coding agent

== Architecture Decision Records

Architecture decision records are generated separately and linked here as a compact index.

[cols="2,4,1,1",options="header"]
|===
|ID |Title |Status |Date
|xref:DECISIONS.adoc#ADR-EMG-001[ADR-EMG-001]
|Generate architecture decision records separately from the main architecture document
|accepted
|2026-04-29
|xref:DECISIONS.adoc#ADR-EMG-002[ADR-EMG-002]
|Keep architecture decision records model-authored and separate from code links
|accepted
|2026-04-29
|===

=== Diagram Color and Shape Legend

This legend applies to all Mermaid diagrams in this document.

[source,mermaid]
----
flowchart LR
  SYS["System"]:::system_boundary
  FG["Functional Group"]:::functional_group
  FU["Functional Unit"]:::functional_unit
  ACT(("Actor")):::actor
  REF["Referenced Element"]:::referenced_element
  IFACE[/"Interface"/]:::interface
  DATA[("Data Object")]:::data_object
  DEPT["Deployment Target"]:::deployment_target
  CTRL[["Control"]]:::control
  TB[/"Trust Boundary"\]:::trust_boundary
  ST(("State")):::state
  EVT(("Event")):::event
  FLOW{"Flow"}:::flow
  FSTEP>"Flow Step"]:::flow_step
  AV(("Attack Vector")):::attack_vector
  REQ["Requirement"]:::requirement
  VER["Verification Check"]:::verification
  RT["Runtime Element"]:::runtime_element
  DEP["Deployment Element"]:::deployment_element
  CODE["Code Element"]:::code_element

  SYS --> FG
  FG --> FU
  ACT --> FU
  FU --> REF
  FU --> IFACE
  FU --> DATA
  FU --> DEPT
  FU --> CTRL
  FU --> TB
  ST -->|triggered_by| EVT
  ST -->|guarded_by| CTRL
  FLOW --> FSTEP
  FSTEP -->|flow_ref| FU
  REQ -->|applies_to| FU
  VER -->|verifies| REQ
  VER -->|implemented_by| CODE
  FU -->|realizes| RT
  DEP --> RT
  AV --> FU
  RT -->|implemented_by| CODE
  REQ -->|code_trace| CODE

classDef functional_group fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#1b5e20,stroke-width:1px,color:#1b5e20;
classDef functional_unit fill:#e3f2fd,stroke:#0d47a1,stroke-width:1px,color:#0d47a1;
classDef actor fill:#fff8e1,stroke:#ef6c00,stroke-width:1px,color:#bf360c;
classDef attack_vector fill:#ffebee,stroke:#b71c1c,stroke-width:1px,color:#7f0000;

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-ARCHITECTURE-INTENT]]
== Architecture Intent View

Show the stable authored architecture intent: capability areas, unit ownership boundaries, and intentional responsibility split.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main capability areas?

- What are the stable units of responsibility and what does each unit own?

- How are responsibilities intentionally split?


=== View-Scoped Projection

[source,mermaid]
----

=== Functional Unit Dependency Diagram

What this diagram shows: dependency paths between functional units (grouped in Functional Group containers) and key referenced elements.
Arrow meaning: `A -->|depends_on| B` means unit `A` requires behavior or data from `B` to fulfill its responsibility.

[source,mermaid]
----
flowchart LR
  subgraph FGBOX_FG_MODEL_AUTHORING["Model Authoring"]
    direction TB
    FU_FU_MODEL_LOADER["Model Loader"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION["CLI Orchestration"]:::functional_unit
  end
  style FGBOX_FG_MODEL_AUTHORING fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#1b5e20,stroke-width:1px;
  subgraph FGBOX_FG_VALIDATION_ANALYSIS["Validation and Analysis"]
    direction TB
    FU_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE["Validation Engine"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_CODEMAP_INFERENCE["Codemap Inference"]:::functional_unit
  end
  style FGBOX_FG_VALIDATION_ANALYSIS fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#1b5e20,stroke-width:1px;
  subgraph FGBOX_FG_ARTIFACT_GENERATION["Artifact Generation"]
    direction TB
    FU_FU_VIEW_PROJECTION["View Projection"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_AI_VIEW_BUILDER["AI View Builder"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR["AsciiDoc Generator"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_THREAT_EXPORTER["Threat Exporter"]:::functional_unit
    FU_FU_STRUCTURIZR_EXPORTER["Structurizr Exporter"]:::functional_unit
  end
  style FGBOX_FG_ARTIFACT_GENERATION fill:#e8f5e9,stroke:#1b5e20,stroke-width:1px;
  subgraph FGBOX_FG_TRACEABILITY_COMPLIANCE["Traceability and Compliance"]
    direction TB

=== Functional Groups and Units (View Scoped)



==== Model Authoring (FG-MODEL-AUTHORING)


Inputs and model loading responsibilities.



Maintains authored architecture, <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirements>>, design, and catalog handling.


















===== CLI Orchestration (FU-CLI-ORCHESTRATION)





Command entrypoints orchestrating model load, validation, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_GENERATION,generation>>, and exports.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION,cli orchestration>>; includes decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_AI_VIEW_BUILDER,AI View Builder>> and decision and orchestration <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>> to <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_AI_VIEW_BUILDER,AI View Builder>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>>, <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>>

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_001,REQ-EMG-001>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_002,REQ-EMG-002>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_003,REQ-EMG-003>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_004,REQ-EMG-004>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_005,REQ-EMG-005>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_006,REQ-EMG-006>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_009,REQ-EMG-009>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_013,REQ-EMG-013>>, <<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_014,REQ-EMG-014>>






===== Model Loader (FU-MODEL-LOADER)





Loads and normalizes architecture, catalog, <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirements>>, and design documents.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

functional responsibility for <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,model loader>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

none

[discrete]
====== Linked Requirements

no explicit authored <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> trigger
















==== Validation and Analysis (FG-VALIDATION-ANALYSIS)


Validation and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_INFERENCE,inference>> responsibilities.



Performs consistency checks and derives runtime, code, and verification evidence.




























===== Codemap Inference (FU-CODEMAP-INFERENCE)





Infers code/runtime ownership and verification links from source and tests.

[discrete]
====== Owned Responsibility

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

[discrete]

<<REF_IDX-REQ_REQ_EMG_010,REQ-EMG-010>>

[discrete]
====== Key Collaborators

[discrete]

==== Artifact Generation (FG-ARTIFACT-GENERATION)


Publication and exchange <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FG_ARTIFACT_GENERATION,artifact generation>>.



Produces AsciiDoc, AI view, and external modeling outputs.

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-SECURITY]]
== Security View

Show inferred exposure and dependency risk points aligned to unit boundaries, focused on attack paths and security evidence.

=== What This View Answers


- What are the main <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_TRUST_BOUNDARY,trust boundaries>> and attack paths?

- Which units are exposed and what security evidence exists?

- Where is the threat model incomplete?


=== View-Scoped Projection

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 3/12 units have direct evidence coverage in this view.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_AI_VIEW_BUILDER,AI View Builder>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>> has no explicit authored attack-vector mapping yet; document technical and fraud/abuse threats even when mitigated.

|TS-MCP-PATH-TRAVERSAL |MCP <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_PATH_TRAVERSAL,path traversal>> accesses non-repo files |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_AV_PATH_TRAVERSAL_IN_MCP,Path Traversal in MCP Calls>> |<<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MCP_SERVER,MCP Server>> |<<REF_IDX-FLOW_FLOW_MODEL_CHANGE_TO_VERIFIED_ARTIFACTS,Model Change to Verified Artifacts Flow>> |medium |high |high

|===

Rejects <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_INVALID,invalid>> parsing <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_STATE,states>> and unresolved core model references.

code modules: model

===== MCP Server (FU-MCP-SERVER)


Enforces strict schemas, panic containment, and repo-root path constraints.


[discrete]
====== Attack Surface

=== Coverage Gaps

Coverage summary: 10/10 units have direct evidence coverage in this view.


- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_AI_VIEW_BUILDER,AI View Builder>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_ASCIIDOC_GENERATOR,AsciiDoc Generator>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CLI_ORCHESTRATION,CLI Orchestration>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_CODEMAP_INFERENCE,Codemap Inference>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_LOBSTER_EXPORTER,LOBSTER Exporter>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MCP_SERVER,MCP Server>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_MODEL_LOADER,Model Loader>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_TRLC_EXPORTER,TRLC Exporter>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VALIDATION_ENGINE,Validation Engine>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.

- <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FU_VIEW_PROJECTION,View Projection>> has no direct inferred runtime evidence yet.


=== Recommended Next Evidence Additions


- Add explicit requirement-to-owner mappings where <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> scope is currently broad or ambiguous.

- Add ownership annotations for runtime and code artifacts where coverage is still unresolved.

- Prioritize closing gaps for units that are authored but lack both runtime and code evidence.

[[SEC_VIEW_VIEW-STATE-LIFECYCLE]]

== Interaction Flow View

Show user-intent-to-outcome causal <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_FLOW,flow>>, including ordered steps, data movement, and error/async branches.

=== What This View Answers


- What happens from user intent to system outcome, step by step?

- What data enters/exits each step and where are decisions made?

- Where are async and error paths and what completes each path?

== Traceability Appendix

=== Requirement Details
[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_001]]
==== REQ-EMG-001

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_MODE_LOCAL_DEVELOPMENT,local development mode is active>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_MODEL_UPDATED,model updated event is received>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall validate <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_ARCHITECTURE_MODEL,architecture model>> before <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>.


NOTE: Validation must gate all <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_GENERATION,generation>> flows.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_007]]
==== REQ-EMG-007

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_MCP_SERVER,mcp server is enabled>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_MCP_TOOL_CALL_RECEIVED,mcp tool call is received>> and <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_COND_CATALOG_REFERENCES_RESOLVE,catalog references resolve successfully>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall return <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_MCP_TOOL_RESULT,mcp tool result>> with schema version and structured error fields.


NOTE: MCP response contract stability <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>>.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_010]]
==== REQ-EMG-010

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_COND_REQUIREMENT_TRACE_COMPLETE,requirement trace is complete>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_MODEL_UPDATED,model updated event is received>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall infer verification links from TRLC-LINKS markers to keep traceability coverage current.


NOTE: Links code/test markers to modeled <<REF_IDX-ENGMODEL_EM_REQUIREMENT,requirement>> coverage.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_011]]
==== REQ-EMG-011

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_COND_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA_AVAILABLE,external schema dependencies are available>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall fail validation if schema checks do not match expected constraints.


NOTE: Protect export integrity when schema trust fails.



===== Requirement-to-Unit-to-Evidence Coverage

What this diagram shows: this requirement-to-unit mapping extended with inferred runtime/code plus verification evidence attached to each requirement and unit.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_012]]
==== REQ-EMG-012

While <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_STATE_MODEL_VALID,model is valid>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall include support paths plus implementation paths plus gaps in <<REF_IDX-DO_DO_AI_JSON_ARTIFACT,ai json artifact>>.


NOTE: AI implementation planning fields must be present and current.

[[REF_REQ_REQ_EMG_014]]
==== REQ-EMG-014

Where <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_FEAT_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS,architecture decision records are authored>>, when <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_EVT_GENERATION_RUN_REQUESTED,generation run is requested>>, the <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_SYS_ENGINEERING_MODEL_GO,engineering model go>> shall publish <<REF_IDX-CATALOG_DATA_ARCHITECTURE_DECISION_RECORDS,architecture decision records document>> linked from AsciiDoc architecture publication output.


NOTE: ADRs are first-class model content but are published separately from the main architecture narrative.
